# Description __

Burned Deer Meat Eating it will damage your health.

# Cooked Deer Meat

# Description __

Cooked Deer Meat. Eating it will restore some health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 1,898  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Diving Mask

# Description __

A Diving Mask. Provides clear vision under water.

Page views: 2,691  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Diving Tank

# Description __

An oxygen tank that enables breathing under water for a period of time. Can be refilled at a workbench.

Page views: 3,521  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Door Closer

# Description __

Auotmatically closes your doors when left open.

Page views: 4,097  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Armored Double Door](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.toptier)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.toptier)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.toptier~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.toptier~history)



# Armored Double Door

# Description __

The armored double door is the highest tier double door and is the best for base defense. Because of its high durability, if the door is placed in a weak wall frame, raiders may target the wall frame instead of the door itself. The door has working hatches and these hatches allow you to see outside of the door and can be shot through in both directions.

# __

# General Information __

  * **Identifier:** 1221063409
  * **Stack Size:** 1
  * **Despawn Time:** 1 hour
  * **HP:** 1000
  * **Upkeep:** 38 HQM
  * **Decay Time:** 12 hours
  * **Recycler Yield:** 13x HQM, 3x Gears



# Blueprint Requirements __

Tool | Requirements  
---|---  
Research Table | Armored Double Door & 500 Scrap  
Workbench Level 3 | 1125 Scrap Total  
  
# Repairing And Durability __

  * **Max Repair Cost:** 8x HQM, 6x Gears

  * **Durability:** For various weapons (e.g., Assault Rifle Explosive 5.56 Rifle Ammo 250, Timed Explosive Charge 3, Rocket 5, etc.)




# Crafting __

## Workbench __

This item needs to be crafted at a Workbench level 3

Items | Quantity  
---|---  
High Quality Metal | X25  
Gears | X5  
  
Page views: 8,927  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Wood Double Door](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.wood)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.wood)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.wood~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/door.double.hinged.wood~history)



# Wood Double Door

# Description __

A Cheap door to secure your base. Its vulnerability to fire and weak explosive resistance makes the door a temporary solution to securing your base. Due to its flaws you should look at upgrading to a higher tier door such as Sheet Metal.

The Wooden Door can take two kinds of locks the basic Key Lock and the Code Lock. To pick up the door, remove any locks and open, hold down the E (USE) key and select 'Pickup'.

Page views: 4,486  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

Medium strength door, vulnerable to explosives.

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Armored Door](/rust/item/door.hinged.toptier)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/door.hinged.toptier)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/door.hinged.toptier~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/door.hinged.toptier~history)



# Armored Door

# Description __

The Armored Door is the highest tier door and is the best option for base defense. It is relatively stronger than stone wall.

  
  
  
  
  
  


# General Information __

  * **Identifier:** 1353298668
  * **Stack Size:** 1
  * **Despawn Time:** 1 hour
  * **HP:** 1000
  * **Upkeep:** 27 HQM
  * **Decay Time:** 12 hours
  * **Recycler Yield:** 10x HQM, 3x Gears



# Blueprint Requirements __

Tool | Requirements  
---|---  
Research Table | Armored Door & 500 Scrap  
Workbench Level 3 | 625 Scrap Total  
  
# Repairing And Durability __

  * **Max Repair Cost:** 7x HQM, 5x Gears

  * **Durability:** For various weapons (e.g., Assault Rifle Explosive 5.56 Rifle Ammo 250, Timed Explosive Charge 3, Rocket 5, Satchel 15, ect.)




# Crafting __

## Workbench __

This item needs to be crafted at a Workbench level 3

Items | Quantity  
---|---  
High Quality Metal | X20  
Gears | X5  
  
# Tips and Strategies __

  * Never put an armored door as your front door to avoid becoming a raiding target.
  * You can add extra security to a vending machine by placing an armored door in front of it.
  * The door can play a large role in underground tunnel bases with the hatch that allows you to see anything in front of you.
  * Requiring 3 Timed Explosive Charge or 5 Rocket to destroy, making it the best level of door in the game.

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/door.hinged.wood~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/door.hinged.wood~history)



# Wooden Door

# Description __

A Cheap door to secure your base. Its vulnerability to fire and weak explosive resistance makes the door a temporary solution to securing your base. Due to its flaws you should look at upgrading to a higher tier door such as Sheet Metal.

The Wooden Door can take two kinds of locks the basic Key Lock and the Code Lock. To pick up the door, remove any locks and open, hold down the E (USE) key and select 'Pickup'.

Page views: 4,960

# Door Key

# Description __

A key to a door, created from a Lock. Keep this item safe, if lost you'll be unable to open the door again!

Page views: 3,038  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Dragon Door Knocker

# Description __

A heavy brass door knocker. You must possess the Steam item to craft this item.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x20 Metal Fragments



## Recycling Output __

  * x10 Metal Fragments

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Drop Box](/rust/item/dropbox)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/dropbox)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/dropbox~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/dropbox~history)



# Drop Box

# Description __

This item can be deployed on walls so that players can input items from the exterior of the building for safe keeping. You can only access the submitted contents of the Drop Box from the rear.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x200 Metal Fragments



## Recycling Output __

  * x100 Metal Fragments



Page views: 6,687  
Updated: This Year

  * [ __History](/rust/item/drumkit~history)



# Junkyard Drum Kit

# Description __

An array of pots, pans and buckets that passes as a serviceable Drum Kit. Three cymbals, some Tom Drums and a Kick Drum means you can easily lay down a beat.

Page views: 3,497  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Duct Tape

# Description __

A versatile adhesive tape reinforced with cloth.

This item is not obtainable in vanilla rust.

Page views: 4,367  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Bronze Egg

# Description __

A Bronze Egg. Open for a surprise or collect 10 to ugprade to a silver egg.

Page views: 4,227  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Painted Egg

# Description __

Some simple painted eggs. Collect 10 to upgrade to a bronze egg

Page views: 2,686

# Silver Egg

# Description __

A Silver Egg. Contains medium level loot, Collect 10 to upgrade to a gold Egg

Page views: 3,391  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Egg Basket

# Description __

An easter egg basket. Equip to pick up eggs during an easter egg hunt with left click. Use right click to throw

Page views: 4,262  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Easter Door Wreath

# Description __

A beautiful, hand crafted Easter themed door wreath. This items requires the Steam Item to be crafted.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x20 Cloth



## Recycling Output __

  * x10 Cloth



Page views: 3,208  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.andswitch~history)



# AND Switch

# Description __

A logic gate that allows eletrical passthrough if BOTH inputs receives power, passthrough amount is the greater of either power source. Usage per unit: 0  (power).

Page views: 5,831  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.large~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.large~history)



# Large Rechargable Battery

# Description __

A Large Rechargable Battery. Must have a minimum charge of 5 seconds to discharge. Can be wired in series. Charging rate is dependant on power in, with a maximum of 80% efficiency.

Page views: 6,952  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __View](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.medium)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.medium~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.medium~history)



# Medium Rechargable Battery

# Description __

A Medium Rechargable Battery. Must have a minimum charge of 5 seconds to discharge. Can be wired in series. Charging rate is dependant on power in, with a maximum of 80% efficiency.

Page views: 5,825  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

[Home](/rust/) / [Small Rechargable Battery](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.small)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.small)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.small~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.battery.rechargable.small~history)



# Small Rechargable Battery

# Description __

A small rechargable battery. Must have a minimum charge of 5 seconds to discharge. Can be wired in series. Charging rate is dependant on power in, with a maximum of 80% efficiency.

Page views: 4,063  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
